msg:Due to heavy rain in Guangdong, we had to cancel our trip to Chaoshan. On May 1, we decided to go to Wuxi. We booked a flight immediately and chose the Diplomat Suite of Suning Hyatt, which has a great location.
The room is more than 150 square meters, spacious, with a good view from the upper floors, comfortable bedding, and especially a separate study room, so the two children can study without interfering with each other.
The hotel is in a great location, surrounded by shopping malls, Xiaolou Lane, and subways, which is very convenient. There is also a Black Pearl One Diamond Restaurant on the 65th floor of the hotel. Since we arrived at the hotel at 7:30 in the evening, we went to the 65th floor for dinner (special Taihu white fish, pickled pork with preserved vegetables, black truffle fried rice, and 10-year-old rice wine), which greatly relieved the fatigue of the journey.
The key point is that all the staff of the hotel are very enthusiastic and respond to the needs of the guests actively and quickly. We originally planned to stay for only one day, but we stayed for 3 days directly.
Next time I come to Wuxi, I will stay here again.

As a Hyatt
The location can be compared with Grand Hyatt, no problem!
The service quality can be compared with Park Hyatt, there is hope!
This needs to be explained in detail: from the front desk to the room service, they are quite good, with a strong sense of service, and they really help you solve the problem. Because we bring children, we hope to add a bed in the bedroom. The overall space of the bedroom is not particularly spacious, but the room service staff even helped us adjust the placement of furniture, making the bedroom layout very comfortable. Breakfast: The hotel has a lot of breakfast seats, and the service is also very good. There are waiters to guide the seats, so you don't have to find a seat yourself in a mess like Xuzhou Suning Hyatt. But Wuxi is a popular tourist city after all, there are too many guests staying in the hotel on weekends, and we have to wait in line around 9:30! Fortunately, I went to have breakfast after 8 o'clock. There are many kinds of breakfast in the hotel, everything you can think of. The unique characteristic variety is Xiaolongbao, which tastes good, but, however, the production capacity is seriously insufficient! Supply and demand are completely out of balance! Basically, every time a batch is steamed, it will be instant. During the two breakfasts during the stay, I only grabbed 6 pieces in total, and I can‚Äôt get enough! It is strongly recommended that the hotel can adjust the production capacity in time according to the number of guests!
Transportation: The hotel is located in the area of Sanyang Square/Chong'an Temple, the most popular commercial center in Wuxi, next to Sanyang Square Station, the largest subway station in China, with a total of 27 entrances and exits. The hotel is only 2 subway stops away from Wuxi Railway Station, and the hotel can be seen from the platform of Wuxi Railway Station. It is very convenient to go to Yuantouzhu, Huishan Ancient Town, Lingshan Giant Buddha, etc. from the hotel. For dinner, there are more than 5 large shopping mall complexes around, as well as the underground commercial street of Sanyang Plaza, as well as many nearby streets, back streets and alleys, and a large number of restaurants and restaurants, it is impossible to choose.
Happy Hour at Regency Club: Located on the 64th floor, with a good view, the first night's food is good, especially the cold fish skin, but the second night is so-so. Compared with the executive lounges of other hotels, Wuxi Suning Hyatt does not have freshly cooked pasta or wonton dumplings.
Overall evaluation: A stunning and impressive Suning Hyatt trip, super full-score experience. If you sort the three Suning Hyatts, Wuxi Suning Hyatt > Town Jiangsu Ning Hyatt > Xuzhou Suning Hyatt, believe me, the 4.5 points shown on Ctrip are definitely underestimated, absolutely!
